home againe god replied king although haue hitherto alwaies inuincible yet ſhall bee ſo farre conſtrained abide comming hither becauſe hee muſt need partake ioy wee haue receiued meanes ſuccour brother thinkes armour much impaired ſince departed camp albeit well aſſured lay ruſting armourie fight laſted betweene men mine ought haue heard brought thus faſhion haue receiued payment beyond
